sally against it because they think these be all of the enemy -- still when he come to the rescue with he whole remain army he both cut he opponent down in open fight and annihilate they by a ambuscade -lrb- -24 - -rrb- while he be thus engage the bastarna cease they flight and remain near the cedrus -lrb- 78 -rrb- river to watch what would take place when after conquer the moesian the roman general start against they they send envoy forbid he to pursue they since they have do the roman no harm crassus detain they say he would give they they answer the follow day and besides treat they kindly he make they drunk so that he learn all they plan the whole scythian race be insatiable in the use of wine and quickly succumb to its influence crassus meanwhile during the night advance to a wood and after station scout in front of the forest make he army stop there thereupon the bastarna think the former be alone make a charge upon they follow they up also when the man retreat into the dense forest and many of the pursuer perish there as well as many other in the flight which follow be obstruct by they wagon which be behind they and owe they defeat further to they desire to save they wife and child they king deldo be slam by crassus himself the armor strip from the prince he would have dedicate as spolium opima to jupiter feretrius have he be a general act on he own authority such be the course of that engagement : of the remainder some take refuge in a grove which be set on fire all around and other leap into a fort where they be annihilate still other perish either by be drive into the ister or after be scatter through the country some survive even yet and occupy a strong post where crassus besiege they in vain for several day then with the aid of role king of some of the getae he destroy they role when he visit caesar be treat as a friend and ally for this assistance : the captive be distribute to the soldier -lrb- -25 - -rrb- after accomplish this crassus turn he attention to the moesian and partly by persuade some of they partly by scare they and partly by the application of force he subjugate all except a very few though with labor and danger temporarily owe to the winter he retire into friendly territory after suffer greatly from the cold and still more at the hand of the thracian through whose country as friendly he be return hence he decide to be satisfy with what he have effect for sacrifice and a triumph have be vote not only to caesar but to he also though accord at least to some account he do not secure the title of imperator but caesar alone might apply it to himself the bastarna however angry at they disaster on learn that he would make no further campaign against they turn again upon the dentheletus and sita whom they regard as have be the chief cause of they evil then crassus though reluctantly take the field and by force march fall upon they unexpectedly conquer and thereafter impose such term as he please now that he have once take up arm again he conceive a desire to recompense the thracian who have harass he during he retreat from moesium for news be bring at this time that they be fortify position and be spoil for a fight and he do subdue they though not without effort by conquer in battle the merdus and the serdus and cut off the hand of the captive he overrun the rest of the country except the land of the odrysae these he spare because they be attach to the service of dionysus and have come to meet he on this occasion without arm also he grant they the piece of land in which they magnify the god and take it away from the bessus who be occupy it -lrb- -26 - -rrb- while he be so occupied he receive a summons from role who have become embroil with dapyx himself also a king of the getae crassus go to help he and by hurl the horse of he opponent back upon the infantry he thoroughly terrify the latter so that he carry the battle no further but cause a great slaughter of the fugitive of both division next he cut off dapyx who have take refuge in a fort and besiege he during the investment some one from the wall salute he in greek and upon obtain a audience arrange to betray the place the barbarian catch in this way turn upon one another and dapyx be kill besides many other he brother however crassus take alive and not only do he no harm but release he at the close of this exploit he lead he army against the cave call keirus the native in great number have occupy this place which be extremely large and so very strong that the tradition obtain that the titan after the defeat administer to they by the god take refuge there here the people have bring together all they flock and they other principal valuable crassus after find all its entrance which be crooked and hard to search out wall they up and in this way subjugate the man by famine upon this success he do not keep he hand from the rest of the getae though they have nothing to do with dapyx he march upon genouclum the most strongly defend fortress of the kingdom of zurax because he hear that the standard which the bastarna have take from gaius antonius near the city of the istrianus be there he assault be make both with the infantry and upon the ister -- the city be near the water -- and in a short time though with much labor in spite of the absence of zurax he take the place the king as soon as he hear of the roman 's approach have set off with money to the scythian to seek a alliance and do not return in time this he do among the getae some of the moesian who have be subdue rise in revolt and they he win back by the energy of other : -lrb- -27 - -rrb- he himself lead a campaign against the artacius and a few other tribe who have never be capture and would not acknowledge he authority pride themselves greatly on this point and imbue the rest with both anger and a disposition to rebel he bring they to term partly by force as they do but little and partly by the fear which the capture of some inspire
